rm -f img.o output.o main.o fail.o input.o compute.o heat_pth2
gcc -O2 -std=gnu99  -pthread -I../../include -c img.c -o img.o 	
gcc -O2 -std=gnu99  -pthread -I../../include -c output.c -o output.o 	
gcc -O2 -std=gnu99  -pthread -I../../include -c main.c -o main.o 	
gcc -O2 -std=gnu99  -pthread -I../../include -c fail.c -o fail.o 	
gcc -O2 -std=gnu99  -pthread -I../../include -c input.c -o input.o 	
gcc -O2 -std=gnu99  -pthread -I../../include -c compute.c -o compute.o

Parameters:
  -n 1000 # number of rows
  -m 1000 # number of columns
  -i 5000 # maximum number of iterations
  -k 70 # reduction period
  -e 1.000000e-06 # convergence threshold
  -c ../../metrics/assignment_2/heat/data/areas_1000x1000.pgm # input file for conductivity
  -t ../../metrics/assignment_2/heat/data/areas_1000x1000.pgm # input file for initial temperatures
  -L 0.000000e+00 # coolest temperature in input/output
  -H 1.000000e+02 # highest temperature in input/output
  -p 1 # number of threads (if applicable)
  -r 0 # print intermediate reports every reduction cycle
